\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The function returns either {\ttfamily ARM\+\_\+\+CMSIS\+\_\+\+NN\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+\+ERROR} if argument constraints fail. or, {\ttfamily ARM\+\_\+\+CMSIS\+\_\+\+NN\+\_\+\+SUCCESS} on successful completion.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function implement convolution with 1x1 kernel size (i.\+e., dim\+\_\+kernel\+\_\+x=1 and dim\+\_\+kernel\+\_\+y=1). It can be used for second half of Mobile\+Nets after depthwise separable convolution.

This function is the version with full list of optimization tricks, but with some contraints\+: ch\+\_\+im\+\_\+in is multiple of 4 ch\+\_\+im\+\_\+out is multiple of 2 \Hypertarget{_face___access__inferencing_2src_2edge-impulse-sdk_2_c_m_s_i_s_2_n_n_2_include_2arm__nnfunctions_8h_a6a218bcb96011379bfe78f08f055cb28}\index{arm\_nnfunctions.h@{arm\_nnfunctions.h}!arm\_convolve\_HWC\_q15\_basic@{arm\_convolve\_HWC\_q15\_basic}}

void arm\+\_\+nn\+\_\+activations\+\_\+direct\+\_\+q15 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_arduino_2_get_started_with_machine_learning_on_arduino_2tflite-micro-arduino-examples-main_2src94b17e0c9eb159f6604b7500918c7321_ab5a8fb21a5b3b983d5f54f31614052ea}{q15\+\_\+t}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{data}{, }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{size}{, }\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{int\+\_\+width}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_arduino_2_get_started_with_machine_learning_on_arduino_2tflite-micro-arduino-examples-main_2srcbed6136de05c6e069de3710a56d1390e_a7f41aa78cd9a0552fae9b348ee4831a0}{arm\+\_\+nn\+\_\+activation\+\_\+type}}}]{type}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Q15 neural network activation function using direct table look-\/up. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em data} & pointer to input \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em size} & number of elements \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em int\+\_\+width} & bit-\/width of the integer part, assume to be smaller than 3 \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em type} & type of activation functions\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This is the direct table look-\/up approach.

Assume here the integer part of the fixed-\/point is \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= 3. More than 3 just not making much sense, makes no difference with saturation followed by any of these activation functions. \Hypertarget{_face___access__inferencing_2src_2edge-impulse-sdk_2_c_m_s_i_s_2_n_n_2_include_2arm__nnfunctions_8h_a79f11131ae6767d60e03b1f6506b1af8}\index{arm\_nnfunctions.h@{arm\_nnfunctions.h}!arm\_nn\_activations\_direct\_q7@{arm\_nn\_activations\_direct\_q7}}

Matrix-\/\+Multiplication Kernels for Convolution. 

These functions are used within convolution layer functions for matrix multiplication.

The implementation is similar to CMSIS-\/\+DSP arm\+\_\+mat\+\_\+mult functions with one Q7 and one Q15 operands. The Q15 operand is the im2col output which is always with 2 columns.

Matrix-\/multiplication function for convolution 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pA} & pointer to operand A \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em p\+In\+Buffer} & pointer to operand B, always conssists of 2 vectors \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em ch\+\_\+im\+\_\+out} & num\+Row of A \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em num\+Col\+\_\+A} & num\+Col of A \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em bias\+\_\+shift} & amount of left-\/shift for bias \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em out\+\_\+shift} & amount of right-\/shift for output \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em bias} & the bias \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in,out}}  & {\em p\+Out} & pointer to output \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The function returns the incremented output pointer 
\end{DoxyReturn}
